The problem is that the guinea pig who's been put on his back, and looks like he's asleep actually isn't having fun! He's terrifying and mimicking a death response because it's what a predator does to disable it's pray and what pray do to in a last ditch effort to persuade the predator that they're not worth eating because there already dead. Rabbits also do it, and no they don't enjoy it, they hate it. They look calm because it's the only option left to them in that situation, and doing that can in extreme cases kill them because of the shock it causes.

Hi guys, So I just started a petition on the Whitehouse site which calls upon congress to make factory farming illegal, and I figured that I would come here for fellow animal lovers. For those of you who don't know, factory farming is the practice of keeping a huge amount of farm animals in a very confined space so as to maximize profit with no concern for the animals. The space in a factory farm is so confined, in fact, that the animals have no room even to move. These animals are bred unnaturally, to have certain profit-increasing enhancements which jeopardize the health of the animals. Often, these farms fail to operate within legal limits of animal welfare and continue to do so unhampered. Factory farming is an incredibly common practice.
So, what I ask of you is to go to my petition and sign it. Maybe if enough of us do it, we can make some sort of difference in this horrible practice.
Here's the link: https://petitions.whitehouse.gov/petition/make-factory-farming-illegal-and-hold-farms-higher-standards-animal-welfare
Thanks!

Yes this is cute, but do people realize that the cute sounds and movements stem from this small animal feeling threatened by having a camera stuck in his face while he's eating? It is called "resource defending behavior" and is a sign is distress in the animal exhibiting it. All these cute videos are the direct result of the person filming essentially terrorizing this animal while he's trying to eat.
